!faqHits.includes(f2)){ faqHits.push(f2); if(faqHits.length>=2)break; }\r }\r for(const f of faqHits.slice(0,2)){\r const faqBody=stripHTML(f.answer)+(f.detail?'\n（补充）'+stripHTML(f.detail):'');\r parts.push('【FAQ · '+f.title+'】（子领域：'+(f.subfield||'通用')+'）\n'+faqBody);\r totalSources++;\r }\r \r /* 2) BM25 KB 检索（�?top 3，含 detail�?*/\r const m=bm25MatchKB(q);\r if(m){\r const chNum=m.entry.chapter?('�?+m.entry.chapter+'�?):'通用';\r parts.push('【KB · '+m.entry.topic+'】（来源：实验手�?KB · '+chNum+'）\n'+(m.entry.answer||'')+((m.entry.detail&&m.entry.detail!==m.entry.answer)?'\n（细节）'+(m.entry.detail||''):''));\r totalSources++;\r if(m.second && m.secondScore >= m.score*0.25){\r parts.push('【KB 补充 · '+m.second.topic+'】\n'+(m.second.answer||'').slice(0,600));\r totalSources++;\r }\r if(m.third && m.thirdScore >= m.score*0.18 && totalSources<4){\r parts.push('【KB 参�?· '+m.third.topic+'】\n'+(m.third.answer||'').slice(0,400));\r totalSources++;\r }\r }\r \r /* 3) Corpus 文献检索（�?top 3，含摘要/方法/对象�?*/\r if(Corpus.loaded && Corpus.entries.length){\r const cr=searchCorpus(q, 4);\r if(cr&&cr.results&&cr.results.length){\r const goodHits=cr.results.filter(r=>r.score>=3);\r for(const r of goodHits.slice(0,3)){\r const lit=[];\r if(r.e.abstract) lit.push('摘要�?+r.e.abstract.slice(0,400));\r if(r.e.methods) lit.push('方法�?+r.e.methods);\r if(r.e.objects) lit.push('对象�?+r.e.objects);\r if(r.e.journal) lit.push('出处�?+r.e.journal+(r.e.doi?' DOI:'+r.e.doi:''));\r parts.push('【文�?· '+r.e.title+'】（相关�?'+r.score+'）\n'+lit.join('�?));\r totalSources++;\r }\r }\r }\r \r /* 4) v7 第二遍回退检索：第一遍未命中时降低阈值再搜一次（FAQ + KB 软匹配） */\r if(totalSources===0){\r /* 4a) KB 软匹配（阈值降至正常的55%，已在bm25MatchKB的soft参数中实现） */\r const m2=bm25MatchKB(q,true);\r if(m2){\r const chNum2=m2.entry.chapter?('�?+m2.entry.chapter+'�?):'通用';\r parts.push('【KB（软匹配）�?'+m2.entry.topic+'】（来源：实验手�?KB · '+chNum2+'）\n'+(m2.entry.answer||'')+((m2.entry.detail&&m2.entry.detail!==m2.entry.answer)?'\n（细节）'+(m2.entry.detail||''):''));\r totalSources++;\r if(m2.second && m2.secondScore >= m2.score*0.3){\r parts.push('【KB 补充 · '+m2.second.topic+'】\n'+(m2.second.answer||'').slice(0,600));\r totalSources++;\r }\r if(m2.third && m2.thirdScore >= m2.score*0.2 && totalSources<3){\r parts.push('【KB 参�?· '+m2.third.topic+'】\n'+(m2.third.answer||'').slice(0,400));\r totalSources++;\r }\r }\r /* 4b) FAQ 回退匹配：降低门槛，仅需命中任意1个非泛化key即可 */\r if(totalSources<3){\r const nq2=norm(q);\r const faqFallback=[];\r for(const f of FAQ){\r let kh=0;\r for(const k of f.keys){\r const nk=norm(k);\r if(nq2.includes(nk) && !FAQ_GENERIC_KEYS.has(nk)){ kh++; }\r }\r for(const en of (f.ents||[])){ if(nq2.includes(norm(en)))kh+=2; }\r if(kh>=1){ faqFallback.push({f,score:kh}); }\r }\r faqFallback.sort((a,b)=>b.score-a.score);\r for(const fb of faqFallback.slice(0,2)){\r const fbBody=stripHTML(fb.f.answer)+(fb.f.detail?'\n（补充）'+stripHTML(fb.f.detail):'');\r parts.push('【FAQ（回退）�?'+fb.f.title+'】（子领域：'+(fb.f.subfield||'通用')+'）\n'+fbBody);\r totalSources++;\r }\r }\r /* 4c) 仍然全部未命�?�?返回空触发联网搜�?*/\r if(totalSources===0) return '';\r }\r \r /* 5) 实验关键参数速查（精密校准数据，LLM回答时优先以此为准） */\r const CHEATSHEET='【实验关键参数速查 �?以下数据回答时以此为准�?\r +'\n基本试剂参数：莫尔盐(NH�?₂Fe(SO�?₂�?H₂O M=392.14 g/mol，浅绿色结晶；产�?K₃[Fe(C₂O�?₃]·3H₂O M=491.25 g/mol，翠绿色单斜晶系晶体；草�?H₂C₂O₄�?H₂O nq=norm(q),terms=new Set(),strong=new Set();\r const addS=t=>{t=norm(t);if(t&&t.length>=2){terms.add(t);strong.add(t);}};\r DOMAIN_TERMS.forEach(t=>{if(nq.includes(norm(t)))addS(t);});\r // 化学实体/同义词扩展：命中一个别�?�?同组全部别名都作为检索词\r CHEM_DB.forEach(c=>{if(c.alias.some(a=>nq.includes(norm(a))))c.alias.forEach(a=>addS(a));});\r (q.toLowerCase().match(/[a-z0-9\[\]\(\)\+\-\.]{2,}/g)||[]).forEach(w=>{if(!STOP_TERMS.includes(w)){terms.add(w);if(/[a-z]/.test(w))strong.add(w);}});\r filt=a=>a.filter(t=>t&&t.length>=2&&!STOP_TERMS.includes(t));\r return {all:filt(Array.from(terms)),strong:new Set(filt(Array.from(strong)))};\r }\r function detectChems(q){const nq=norm(q);return CHEM_DB.filter(c=>c.alias.some(a=>nq.includes(norm(a))));}\r function detectOps(q){const nq=norm(q);return OP_TERMS.filter(o=>nq.includes(norm(o)));}\r \r function searchCorpus(q,topN){\r const {all,strong}=extractTerms(q);\r if(!all.length||!Corpus.entries.length) return {terms:all,results:[]};\r const nq=norm(q);\r const boosts=CONCEPT_BOOST.filter(b=>b.keys.some(k=>nq.includes(norm(k))));\r const out=[];\r for(const e of Corpus.entries){\r const f={\r title:norm(e.title),subfield:norm(e.subfield),objects:norm(e.objects),methods:norm(e.methods),\r questions:norm((e.questions||[]).join('|')),content:norm(e.content||''),abstract:norm(e.abstract||'')\r };\r let s=0,sh=false;const hit=new Set();\r for(const t of all){\r let w=0;\r if(f.questions.includes(t))w=Math.max(w,10);\r if(f.title.includes(t))w=Math.max(w,6);\r if(f.content&&f.content.includes(t))w=Math.max(w,6);\r if(f.objects.includes(t)||f.methods.includes(t))w=Math.max(w,4);\r if(f.abstract.includes(t))w=Math.max(w,4);\r if(f.subfield.includes(t))w=Math.max(w,3);\r if(w>0){s+=w;hit.add(t);if(strong.has(t))sh=true;}\r }\r for(const b of boosts){ if(f.subfield===norm(b.sub)){ s+=b.bonus; sh=true; hit.add('领域:'+b.sub);} }\r if(s>0) out.push({e,score:s,hit:Array.from(hit),strongHit:sh});\r }\r out.sort((a,b)=>b.score-a.score);\r return {terms:all,results:out.slice(0,topN||6)};\r }\r const HIT_THRESHOLD=6;\r /* while((cm=cr.exec(after))!==null)result.options.push({letter:map[cm[1]],text:cm[2].trim()});\r return result;\r }\r }\r \r /* 2c: 括号字母标记 (A) (B) ... */\r const parenIdx=q.search(/[\(（][A-H][\)）]/);\r cleanQ=q.slice(0,parenIdx).trim().replace(/[�?。！!�?\s]+$/,'');\r if(cleanQ.length<4)cleanQ=q;\r result.cleanQuery=cleanQ;\r const pr=/[\(（]([A-H])[\)）]\s*(.+?)(?=\s*[\(（][A-H][\)）]|$)/g;\r let pm;\r while((pm=pr.exec(after))!==null)result.options.push({letter:pm[1],text:pm[2].trim()});\r return result;\r }\r }\r \r /* 2d: 数字标记 1. 2. 3. …（至少3个才视为选项�?*/\r const numIdx=q.search(/(?:^|\s|。|\?|�?(\d+)[\.\．、]/);\r if(numIdx>0){\r const after=q.slice(numIdx+1);\r const nm=(after.match(/(?:^|\s+)(\d+)[\.\．、]\s*\S/g)||[]);\r if(nm.length>=3){\r result.isTest=true;\r result.isMultiChoice=true;\r const letters='ABCDEFGH';\r let cleanQ=q.slice(0,numIdx+1).trim().replace(/[�?。！!�?\s]+$/,'');\r if(cleanQ.length<4)cleanQ=q;\r if(/^(下列|以下|下面|下述).*(正确|错误|有误|不符|恰当|准确|合理|可行|如实|符合).*[的是]/i.test(q)||\r /^(下列|以下|下面|下述).*(属于|不属�?.*[的是]/i.test(q)||\r /^(关于|对于).*说法.*(正确|错误).*[的是]/i.test(q)||\r /^(下列|以下).*�?*(正确|不正确|错误)/i.test(q)||\r /^(下列|以下).*叙述.*(正确|不正确|错误)/i.test(q)){\r result.isTest=true;\r }\r \r return result;\r }\r \r /* ================= 判断题调�?v4：扩充前缀检�?+ FAQ/BM25/KB三重比对 ================= */\r function qaDetectTrueFalse(q,testInfo){\r if(!testInfo||!testInfo.isTrueFalse)return {handled:false,answer:''};\r let stmt=testInfo.trueFalseStatement;\r /* v4: 更全面的T/F前缀剥离 */\r {handled:true,answer:'该说法错误�?+sj.reason};\r }\r }\r \r /* v4: 2) FAQ 搜索 —�?检查FAQ是否有直接相关的真假判断 */\r const faqHit=matchFAQ(stmt);\r if(faqHit&&faqHit.answer){\r const faqAns=faqHit.answer;\r const for(const t of stmtTerms){if(nsNorm.includes(t))overlap++;}\r if(overlap>=2){contraHits+=overlap;}\r }\r /* 检查FAQ中是否有肯定陈述句与陈述匹配 */\r const result;\r }\r \r /* 辅助：规范化中文标点（全角→半角，保留换行） */\r function normalizeLine(s){return String(s||'').replace(/[：]/g,':').replace(/[，]/g,',').replace(/[。]/g,'.');}\r \r /* LLM 模式的主入口（异步）—�?RAG 制备实验（原理、试剂、操作、产率、误差、安全、表征与拓展应用），该问题超出了我的知识范围，请换用与实验相关的问题提问�?;\r }\r /* 3) 软匹配兜底（加改写兜底） */\r let ms=bm25MatchKB(searchQ,true);\r if(!ms){\r const variants=qaReformulate(searchQ);\r for(const vq of qaFinalizeOutput(qaAssemble(searchQ,ms),testInfo,searchQ);\r }\r return '该问题暂未在本实验知识库中找到确切答案。本实验涉及三草酸合铁酸钾的制备原理、四步操作、产率计算、配合物性质、光化学与安全规范，建议补充更具体的实验关键词（�?氧化温度""结晶�?"产率计算"）再提问�?;\r };\r \r /* 答案后处理：选择题回填选项字母 + 去噪（v4: 多重匹配策略�?*/\r function qaFinalizeOutput(out,testInfo,searchQ){\r if(!testInfo||!testInfo.isMultiChoice||!testInfo.options.length)return out;\r const ansNorm=norm(out);\r const ansLower=out.toLowerCase();\r let bestLetter='',bestScore=0;\r const scores={}; /* 每个选项的累计得�?*/\r for(const opt of testInfo.options)scores[opt.letter]=0;\r \r /* ── 策略1: 精确匹配（选项完整文本出现在答案中�?── */\r for(const opt of testInfo.options){\r const optNorm=norm(opt.text);\r if(!optNorm||optNorm.length<2)continue;\r if(ansNorm.includes(optNorm)){\r scores[opt.letter]+=optNorm.length*3; /* 长度加权，越长越可信 */\r }\r }\r \r /* ── 策略2: 词级匹配（选项文本中的关键词在答案中出现） ── */\r for(const opt of testInfo.options){\r const words=opt.text.split(/[\s�?、；;。．.\(\)（）]+/).filter(w=>w.length>=2);\r if(!words.length)continue;\r let hits=0;\r for(const w of words){\r const wn=norm(w);\r if(wn.length>=2&&ansNorm.includes(wn))hits++;\r }\r const frac=hits/words.length;\r if(frac>=0.5)scores[opt.letter]+=frac*10+Math.floor(hits*2);\r /* 所有选项都有微小匹配时，以最高分者为�?*/\r scores[opt.letter]+=frac*2;\r }\r \r /* ── 策略3: 双字词对（bigram）重�?── */\r if(!bestLetter||bestScore<5){\r for(const opt of testInfo.options){\r const optNorm=norm(opt.text);\r if(optNorm.length<3)continue;\r const bg=new Set();\r for(let i=0;i<optNorm.length-1;i++){\r const pair=optNorm.substring(i,i+2);\r if(/^[一-鿿\d\w]{2}$/.test(pair))bg.add(pair);\r }\r if(bg.size===0)continue;\r let intersect=0;\r for(const b of bg){if(ansNorm.includes(b))intersect++;}\r const frac=intersect/bg.size;\r scores[opt.letter]+=frac*15;\r }\r }\r \r /* ── 策略4: 关键词提取（选最突出的关键词�?── */\r for(const opt of testInfo.options){\r const optNorm=norm(opt.text);\r /* 提取化学式、数字、特殊ID等强特征�?*/\r const chemMatch=opt.text.match(/[A-Z][a-z]?\d*(?:[A-Z][a-z]?\d*)*/g)||[];\r const numMatch=opt.text.match(/\d+(?:\.\d+)?/g)||[];\r const strongTerms=[...chemMatch,...numMatch];\r let strongHits=0;\r for(const t of strongTerms){\r if(t.length>=2&&ansLower.includes(t.toLowerCase()))strongHits++;\r }\r if(strongTerms.length>0)scores[opt.letter]+=(strongHits/strongTerms.length)*20;\r /* 中文关键词：长度>=3的非停用�?*/\r const zhWords=opt.text.match(/[一-鿿]{3,}/g)||[];\r let zhHits=0;\r for(const zw of zhWords){\r if(ansNorm.includes(norm(zw)))zhHits++;\r }\r if(zhWords.length>0)scores[opt.letter]+=(zhHits/zhWords.length)*12;\r }\r \r /* ── 策略5: 对于"xxx是A还是B�?类问题，检查答案是否明确提及某选项内容 ── */\r const abRe=/(?:是|为|属于|�?([A-H])\s*(?:还是|或|而不�?/i;\r const abMatch=q&&q.match ? String(q).match(abRe) : null;\r if(abMatch&&ansNorm.includes(norm(String(q)))){\r /* 题干本身含选项字母，尝试答案中找对应文�?*/\r for(const opt of testInfo.options){\r if(ansNorm.includes(norm(opt.text)))scores[opt.letter]+=25;\r }\r }\r \r /* ── 策略6: 检查答案是否直接提到选项字母 ── */\r for(const opt of testInfo.options){\r const letterPatterns=[\r new RegExp('选项\\s*'+opt.letter),\r new RegExp('选\\s*'+opt.letter),\r new RegExp('答案[为是]\\s*'+opt.letter),\r new RegExp('[（\\(]\\s*'+opt.letter+'\\s*[）\\)]'),\r new RegExp('故\\s*'+opt.letter),\r ];\r for(const pat of letterPatterns){\r if(pat.test(out)){scores[opt.letter]+=50;break;}\r }\r }\r \r /* ── 汇总判定：选得分最高且领先�?名足够多的选项 ── */\r const entries=Object.entries(scores).filter(([,v])=>v>0).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]);\r if(entries.length>=1){\r const top=entries[0];\r const second=entries.length>=2?entries[1][1]:0;\r /* 第一名得分必须领先第2名至�?分，且总分>=4才认�?*/\r if(top[1]>=4&&(top[1]-second)>=3){\r bestLetter=top[0];bestScore=top[1];\r }else if(top[1]>=8&&entries.length===1){\r /* 仅一个选项有分且足够高 */\r bestLetter=top[0];bestScore=top[1];\r }\r }\r \r /* 回退：最佳精确匹�?*/\r if(!bestLetter){\r for(const opt of testInfo.options){\r const optNorm=norm(opt.text);\r if(!optNorm||optNorm.length<1)continue;\r if(ansNorm.includes(optNorm)){\r const sc=optNorm.length;\r if(sc>bestScore){bestScore=sc;bestLetter=opt.letter;}\r }\r }\r }\r \r /* 若答案中已含"选项"/"答案"字样则不重复追加 */\r if(bestLetter&&!/正确选项|正确答案|故选|故答案为/.test(out)){\r out+='\n\n故正确答案为 '+bestLetter;\r }\r return out;\r }\r /* 版本切换：__qaCore 默认指向 v8，v7 保留用于回退对比 */\r window.__qaCoreV7=window.__qaCore;\r window.__qaCore=window.__qaCoreLLM; /* v5: LLM 优先，本地后�?*/\r \r /* ================= 问答 Tab ================= */\r const QA_KEY='chemai_qa_history';\r const qaChat=$('#qaChat'),qaInput=$('#qaInput'),qaSend=$('#qaSend');\r let qaBusy=false;\r \r function scrollChat(el){el.scrollTop=el.scrollHeight;}\r function addMsg(chatEl,role,html,save){\r const
